목표 : 신규고객 및 이탈 방지 필요 고객 분류에 활용한다

## Load Data and Check

온라인 공개 데이터 중 활용도 있는 연구에 적합한 데이터셋이 없고, 
샘플링, Generator를 통하여 데이터를 생성하여 해당 연구에 활용. 
RAW DATA를 아래와 같이 변환하여 사용하였습니다.

1. Re-Sampling & Rescaling & Randomize 하였습니다.
2. 결제금액, 판매수량 데이터를 표준 정규 분포(Standard Distribution)에 따라 재분배하였습니다.


```python
df = pd.read_csv("sample_and_randomed_scaled.csv", sep=",", low_memory=False )
```


```python
df["고객번호"] = df["고객번호"].astype("str")
df["주문번호"] = df["주문번호"].astype("str")
```

# Pre-Processing (DATA LOAD)

데이터 전체적인 형태를 체크하기 위해 
1. 판매일자 데이터 형식을 통해, Year, Month, Day로 분류
2. NA 데이터 삭제
3. 나이대 데이터 생성


```python
#데이터 전처리
def preprocessing(df):
    s=pd.to_datetime(df['판매일자'],format='%Y%m%d')
    df["Year"], df["Month"], df["Day"] = s.dt.year, s.dt.month, s.dt.day
    df = df.dropna()
    bins = list(range(10,100,10))
    bins
    bins_lable = [str(x)+"대" for x in bins]
    bins_lable
    df["나이대"] = pd.cut(df["나이"], bins, right=False, labels = bins_lable[:-1])
    return df

df = preprocessing(df)
```


```python
dfdf = df[df["나이대"]==np.nan]
```

```python
def check_df(dataframe, head=5):
    print(" SHAPE ".center(70,'#'))
    print('Rows: {}'.format(dataframe.shape[0]))
    print('Columns: {}'.format(dataframe.shape[1]))
    print(" TYPES ".center(70,'#'))
    print(dataframe.dtypes)
    print(" HEAD ".center(70,'#'))
    print(dataframe.head(head))
    print(" TAIL ".center(70,'#'))
    print(dataframe.tail(head))
    print(" MISSING VALUES ".center(70,'#'))
    print(dataframe.isnull().sum())
    print(" QUANTILES ".center(70,'#'))
    print(dataframe.quantile([0, 0.05, 0.50, 0.95, 0.99, 1]).T)
    
check_df(df)
```

```python
today_date = dt.datetime(2021,11,1) #데이터 추출 기준 11월 마감 기준 (회사 정책으로 인함)
```

# RFM Analysis

고객 판매 데이터를 기준으로 Recency, Frequency, Monetary 데이터 생성 및 
RFM 필드를 활용하여 아래 구분을 기준으로 고객 Segmentation 실시

<고객 Segment 기준>

'휴면고객' : 긴 시간 접속이력이 없어, 휴면상태에 들어간 고객

'이탈위험고객' : 서비스에서 이탈될 확률이 높은 고객

'이탈 방지 필요 고객' : 서비스에 이탈하기 이전에 적절한 마케팅 커뮤니케이션이 필요한 고객

'휴면 가능 고객' : 휴면 상태에 들어갈 수 있는 고객

'주의 필요 고객' : 주의 깊게 마케팅을 한다면, 충성 및 우수고객이 될 가능성이 높은 고객

'충성 고객' : 서비스에 충성도가 높은 고객 

'우수 고객' : 판매 실적이 높은 고객

'신규 고객' : 서비스에 신규로 인입된 고객

'충성 고객 후보군' : 충성 고객이 될 가능성이 높은 고객

'VVIP 고객' : VVIP 고객


```python
rfm = df.groupby("고객번호").agg({'OrderDate' : lambda order_date : (today_date - order_date.max()).days,
                                  'OrderNum' : lambda order_num : order_num.nunique(),
                                  'PriceTTL' : lambda price_ttl : price_ttl.sum()}) 
```


```python
rfm.columns = ['recency','frequency','monetary']
rfm = rfm.reset_index()
rfm.head()
```

```python
rfm['recency_score'] = pd.qcut(rfm['recency'],5,labels=[5,4,3,2,1])

rfm['frequency_score'] = pd.qcut(rfm['frequency'].rank(method="first"),5,labels=[1,2,3,4,5])

rfm['monetary_score'] = pd.qcut(rfm['monetary'],5,labels=[1,2,3,4,5])

rfm['RFM_SCORE'] = (rfm['recency_score'].astype(str)+ rfm['frequency_score'].astype(str))
```

# RFM 분류를 통한 고객 세그먼트 나누기


```python
seg_map = {r'[1-2][1-2]': '휴면고객',
           r'[1-2][3-4]': '이탈위험고객',
           r'[1-2]5': '이탈 방지 필요 고객',
           r'3[1-2]': '휴면 가능 고객',
           r'33': '주의 필요 고객',
           r'[3-4][4-5]': '충성 고객',
           r'41': '우수 고객',
           r'51': '신규 고객',
           r'[4-5][2-3]': '충성 고객 후보군',
           r'5[4-5]': 'VVIP 고객'}

rfm['segment'] = rfm['RFM_SCORE'].replace(seg_map, regex=True)
rfm.head()
```

```python
data = go.Bar(y = pd.DataFrame(rfm['segment'].value_counts()).index,
              x = pd.DataFrame(rfm['segment'].value_counts())['segment'].values,
              name = str(pd.DataFrame(rfm['segment'].value_counts())['segment'].values),
              orientation='h')

layout = go.Layout(title={'text': "Number of Customer by Segments",
                          'y':0.9,
                          'x':0.5,
                          'xanchor': 'center',
                          'yanchor': 'top'},
                   xaxis =dict(title='Customers'),
                   template = 'plotly_white')

fig=go.Figure(data=data, layout=layout)
fig.update_xaxes(range=[0,30000])
iplot(fig)
```

```python
fig = go.Figure()
for i in rfm['segment'].unique():
    fig.add_trace(go.Scatter(x=rfm[rfm['segment']==i]['recency'],
                           y=rfm[rfm['segment']==i]['frequency'],
```

            Plotly.purge(gd);

```python
merge1 = pd.merge(left = rfm, right = df, how ="left", on="고객번호")
merge1["sex_code"] = [0 if s == "MALE" else 1 for s in merge1["성별구분"]]
merge1["NEED_ALERT_COL"] = [1 if s == "이탈 방지 필요 고객" else 0 for s in merge1["segment"]]
```



```python
target_data_for_ml = merge1[["recency","frequency","monetary","나이","sex_code","NEED_ALERT_COL"]]
```


```python
NO_NEED_ALERT, NEED_ALERT = np.bincount(target_data_for_ml['NEED_ALERT_COL'])
```


```python
total = NEED_ALERT + NO_NEED_ALERT
```


```python
print('Examples:\n    Total: {}\n    NEED_ALERT: {} ({:.2f}% of total)\n'.format(
    total, NEED_ALERT, 100 * NEED_ALERT / total))
```

        Total: 700000

# Train / Test Data-Set 으로 나누기


```python
X = target_data_for_ml.drop(['NEED_ALERT_COL'], axis=1)
y = target_data_for_ml['NEED_ALERT_COL']
```


```python
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size = 0.3, random_state = 0)
```


```python
X_train.shape, X_test.shape
```




    ((490000, 5), (210000, 5))




```python
categorical = [col for col in X_train.columns if X_train[col].dtypes == 'O']
numerical = [col for col in X_train.columns if X_train[col].dtypes != 'O']
```


```python
import category_encoders as ce
```


```python
encoder = ce.OneHotEncoder(cols=['sex_code'])
```


```python
X_train = encoder.fit_transform(X_train)
X_test = encoder.transform(X_test)
```


```python
X_train.shape
```




    (490000, 6)




```python
X_test.shape
```




    (210000, 6)




```python
cols = X_train.columns
```


```python
from sklearn.preprocessing import RobustScaler
scaler = RobustScaler()
X_train = scaler.fit_transform(X_train)
X_test = scaler.transform(X_test)
```


```python
X_train = pd.DataFrame(X_train, columns=[cols])
X_test = pd.DataFrame(X_test, columns=[cols])
```


```python
y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype="|S6")
```


```python
y_test = np.asarray(y_test, dtype="|S6")
```


```python
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
rfc = RandomForestClassifier(random_state=0)
rfc.fit(X_train, y_train)
y_pred = rfc.predict(X_test)
```


```python
from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score
print('accuracy score : {0:0.4f}'. format(accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred)))
```

    accuracy score : 1.0000
    


```python
from sklearn import tree
import mglearn
```

# Random Forest 의사결정나무 Estimator 100 학습 


```python
rfc_100 = RandomForestClassifier(n_estimators=100, random_state=0)
rfc_100.fit(X_train, y_train)
```




    RandomForestClassifier(random_state=0)




```python
RandomForestClassifier(bootstrap=True, class_weight=None, criterion='gini',
                       max_depth=None, max_features='auto', max_leaf_nodes=None,
                       min_impurity_decrease=0.0,
                       min_samples_leaf=1, min_samples_split=2,
                       min_weight_fraction_leaf=0.0, n_estimators=100,
                       n_jobs=None, oob_score=False, random_state=0, verbose=0,
                       warm_start=False)
```




    RandomForestClassifier(random_state=0)




```python
y_pred_100 = rfc_100.predict(X_test)
```


```python
print(' accuracy score : {0:0.4f}'. format(accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred_100)))
```

     accuracy score : 1.0000

# Tensorflow Binary Classification 분류 기법 적용


```python
target_data_for_ml["recency"] =target_data_for_ml["recency"].astype('float64')
target_data_for_ml["frequency"] =target_data_for_ml["frequency"].astype('float64')
target_data_for_ml["monetary"] =target_data_for_ml["monetary"].astype('float64')
target_data_for_ml["sex_code"] =target_data_for_ml["sex_code"].astype('float64')
target_data_for_ml["NEED_ALERT_COL"] =target_data_for_ml["NEED_ALERT_COL"].astype('object')
```


```python
train_df, test_df = train_test_split(target_data_for_ml, test_size=0.2)
train_df, val_df = train_test_split(train_df, test_size=0.2)
```


```python
train_labels = np.asarray(train_df.pop('NEED_ALERT_COL')).astype('float32')
bool_train_labels = train_labels != 0
val_labels = np.asarray(val_df.pop('NEED_ALERT_COL')).astype('float32')
test_labels = np.asarray(test_df.pop('NEED_ALERT_COL')).astype('float32')
train_features = np.asarray(train_df).astype('float32')
val_features = np.array(val_df).astype('float32')
test_features = np.array(test_df).astype('float32')
```


```python
#Feature 간 스케일링 
scaler = StandardScaler()
train_features = scaler.fit_transform(train_features)
val_features = scaler.transform(val_features)
test_features = scaler.transform(test_features)
train_features = np.clip(train_features, -5, 5)
val_features = np.clip(val_features, -5, 5)
test_features = np.clip(test_features, -5, 5)
print('Training labels shape:', train_labels.shape)
print('Validation labels shape:', val_labels.shape)
print('Test labels shape:', test_labels.shape)
print('Training features shape:', train_features.shape)
print('Validation features shape:', val_features.shape)
print('Test features shape:', test_features.shape)
```

    Training labels shape: (448000,)
    Validation labels shape: (112000,)
    Test labels shape: (140000,)
    Training features shape: (448000, 5)
    Validation features shape: (112000, 5)
    Test features shape: (140000, 5)
    


```python
NEED_ALERT_DF = pd.DataFrame(train_features[ bool_train_labels], columns=train_df.columns)
NO_NEED_ALERT_DF = pd.DataFrame(train_features[~bool_train_labels], columns=train_df.columns)
```

# 데이터 분포 확인하기


```python
#데이터 분포 체크 
#이탈 방지 필요 고객
sns.jointplot(NEED_ALERT_DF['recency'], NEED_ALERT_DF['monetary'],
              kind='hex', xlim=(-3,3), ylim=(-3,3))
plt.suptitle("NEED ALERT distribution")
#이탈 방지 미필요 고객
sns.jointplot(NO_NEED_ALERT_DF['recency'], NO_NEED_ALERT_DF['monetary'],
              kind='hex', xlim=(-3,3), ylim=(-3,3))
_ = plt.suptitle("NO NEED ALERT distribution")
```


    
![png](output_90_0.png)
    



    
![png](output_90_1.png)
    



```python
# 알고리즘 성능 평가 METRICS
METRICS = [
      keras.metrics.TruePositives(name='tp'),
      keras.metrics.FalsePositives(name='fp'),
      keras.metrics.TrueNegatives(name='tn'),
      keras.metrics.FalseNegatives(name='fn'), 
      keras.metrics.BinaryAccuracy(name='accuracy'),
      keras.metrics.Precision(name='precision'),
      keras.metrics.Recall(name='recall'),
      keras.metrics.AUC(name='auc'),
      keras.metrics.AUC(name='prc', curve='PR'), # precision-recall curve
]
```


```python
#모델 구성
def modeling(metrics=METRICS, output_bias=None):
  if output_bias is not None:
    output_bias = tf.keras.initializers.Constant(output_bias)
  model = keras.Sequential([
      keras.layers.Dense(
          16, activation='relu',
          input_shape=(train_features.shape[-1],)),
      keras.layers.Dropout(0.5),
      keras.layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid',
                         bias_initializer=output_bias),
  ])

  model.compile(
      optimizer=keras.optimizers.Adam(learning_rate=1e-3),
      loss=keras.losses.BinaryCrossentropy(),
      metrics=metrics)

  return model
```


```python
#모델 Configuration
EPOCHS = 100
BATCH_SIZE = 2048

early_stopping = tf.keras.callbacks.EarlyStopping(
    monitor='val_auc', 
    verbose=1,
    patience=10,
    mode='max',
    restore_best_weights=True)
```


```python
#모델 Summary
model = modeling()
model.summary()
```

    Model: "sequential_14"

     dense_29 (Dense)            (None, 1)                 17        
                                                                     
    =================================================================
    Total params: 113
    Trainable params: 113
    Non-trainable params: 0
    _________________________________________________________________

# Initial weight 처리


```python
initial_weights = os.path.join(tempfile.mkdtemp(), 'initial_weights')
model.save_weights(initial_weights)
```


```python
model = modeling()
model.load_weights(initial_weights)
model.layers[-1].bias.assign([0.0])
zero_bias_history = model.fit(
    train_features,
    train_labels,
    batch_size=BATCH_SIZE,
    epochs=20,
    validation_data=(val_features, val_labels), 
    verbose=0)
```


```python
model = modeling()
model.load_weights(initial_weights)
careful_bias_history = model.fit(
    train_features,
    train_labels,
    batch_size=BATCH_SIZE,
    epochs=20,
    validation_data=(val_features, val_labels), 
    verbose=0)
```


```python
#loss PLOT
def plot_loss(history, label):
  plt.semilogy(history.epoch, history.history['loss'],
               color='green', label='Train '+label)
  plt.semilogy(history.epoch, history.history['val_loss'],
          color='blue', label='Val '+label,
          linestyle="--")
  plt.xlabel('Epoch')
  plt.ylabel('Loss')

  plt.legend()
```


```python
plot_loss(zero_bias_history, "Zero Bias")
plot_loss(careful_bias_history, "Careful Bias")
```

```python
#Precision and Loss Plot
def plot_metrics(history):
  metrics = ['loss', 'auc', 'precision', 'recall']
  for n, metric in enumerate(metrics):
    name = metric.replace("_"," ").capitalize()
    plt.subplot(2,2,n+1)
    plt.plot(history.epoch, history.history[metric], color="green", label='Train')
    plt.plot(history.epoch, history.history['val_'+metric],
             color="blue", linestyle="--", label='Val')
    plt.xlabel('Epoch')
    plt.ylabel(name)
    if metric == 'loss':
      plt.ylim([0, plt.ylim()[1]])
    elif metric == 'auc':
      plt.ylim([0.8,1])
    else:
      plt.ylim([0,1])

    plt.legend()
```


```python
plot_metrics(baseline_history)
```

```python
#Confusion Matrix plotting 함수
def plot_cm(labels, predictions, p=0.5):
  cm = confusion_matrix(labels, predictions > p)
  plt.figure(figsize=(5,5))
  sns.heatmap(cm, annot=True, fmt="d")
  plt.title('MATRIX @{:.2f}'.format(p))
  plt.ylabel('실제 LABEL')
  plt.xlabel('예측된 LABEL')

  print('이탈 방지 미필요 고객 정분류 (True Negatives): ', cm[0][0])
  print('이탈 방지 미필요 고객 오분류 (False Positives): ', cm[0][1])
  print('이탈 방지 필요 고객 오분류 (False Negatives): ', cm[1][0])
  print('이탈 방지 필요 고객 정분류 (True Positives): ', cm[1][1])
  print('이탈 방지 필요 고객 Total: ', np.sum(cm[1]))
```


```python

                                  batch_size=BATCH_SIZE, verbose=0)

  print(name, ': ', value)
print()
```

```python
#ROC plotting 함수
def plot_roc(name, labels, predictions, **kwargs):
  fp, tp, _ = sklearn.metrics.roc_curve(labels, predictions)
  plt.plot(100*fp, 100*tp, label=name, linewidth=2, **kwargs)
  plt.xlabel('False positives [%]')
  plt.ylabel('True positives [%]')
  plt.xlim([-0.5,20])
  plt.ylim([80,100.5])
  plt.grid(True)
  ax = plt.gca()
  ax.set_aspect('equal')
```


```python
plot_roc("Train Baseline", train_labels, train_predictions_baseline, color="blue")
plot_roc("Test Baseline", test_labels, test_predictions_baseline, color="green", linestyle='--')
plt.legend(loc='lower right')
```




    <matplotlib.legend.Legend at 0x1cc0afdba88>

```python
#PRC plotting 함수
def plot_prc(name, labels, predictions, **kwargs):
    precision, recall, _ = sklearn.metrics.precision_recall_curve(labels, predictions)
    plt.plot(precision, recall, label=name, linewidth=2, **kwargs)
    plt.xlabel('Recall')
    plt.ylabel('Precision')
    plt.xlim([-0,1.2]) #1에 붙은 그래프 보정
    plt.ylim([-0,1.2])
    plt.grid(True)
    ax = plt.gca()
    ax.set_aspect('equal')
```


```python
plot_prc("Train Baseline", train_labels, train_predictions_baseline, color="green")
plot_prc("Test Baseline", test_labels, test_predictions_baseline, color="blue", linestyle='--')
plt.legend(loc='lower right')
```

```python
NEED_ARERT_FEATURES = train_features[bool_train_labels]
NO_NEED_ARERT_FEATURES = train_features[~bool_train_labels]

NEED_ARERT_LABELS = train_labels[bool_train_labels]
NO_NEED_ARERT_LABELS = train_labels[~bool_train_labels]
```


```python
ids = np.arange(len(NEED_ARERT_FEATURES))
choices = np.random.choice(ids, len(NO_NEED_ARERT_FEATURES))

RES_NEED_ARERT_FEATURES = NEED_ARERT_FEATURES[choices]
RES_NEED_ARERT_LABELS = NEED_ARERT_LABELS[choices]

RES_NEED_ARERT_FEATURES.shape
```




    (431549, 5)




```python
#Re-Sampling 후
resampled_features = np.concatenate([RES_NEED_ARERT_FEATURES, NO_NEED_ARERT_FEATURES], axis=0)
resampled_labels = np.concatenate([RES_NEED_ARERT_LABELS, NO_NEED_ARERT_LABELS], axis=0)

order = np.arange(len(resampled_labels))
np.random.shuffle(order)
resampled_features = resampled_features[order]
resampled_labels = resampled_labels[order]

resampled_features.shape
```




    (863098, 5)




```python
BUFFER_SIZE = 100000

def make_dataset(features, labels):
  dataset = tf.data.Dataset.from_tensor_slices((features, labels))#.cache()
  dataset = dataset.shuffle(BUFFER_SIZE).repeat()
  return dataset

NEED_ARERT_DS = make_dataset(NEED_ARERT_FEATURES, NEED_ARERT_LABELS)
NO_NEED_ARERT_DS = make_dataset(NO_NEED_ARERT_FEATURES, NO_NEED_ARERT_LABELS)
```


```python
for features, label in NEED_ARERT_DS.take(1):
  print("Features:\n", features.numpy())
  print()
  print("Label: ", label.numpy())
```

```python
# 가중치 50% , 50% 으로 훈련데이터 Re-sampling
resampled_dataset = tf.data.experimental.sample_from_datasets([NEED_ARERT_DS, NO_NEED_ARERT_DS], weights=[0.5, 0.5])
resampled_dataset = resampled_dataset.batch(BATCH_SIZE).prefetch(2)
```

```python
for features, label in resampled_dataset.take(1):
```

```python
output_layer.bias.assign([0])

    resampled_ds,
    epochs=EPOCHS,
    steps_per_epoch=resampled_steps_per_epoch,

    validation_data=val_ds)
```

```python
resampled_model = modeling()
#Initial weight 적용
resampled_model.load_weights(initial_weights)

#Output Layer Bias 
output_layer = resampled_model.layers[-1] 
output_layer.bias.assign([0])

resampled_history = resampled_model.fit(
    resampled_ds,
    steps_per_epoch=20,
    epochs=10*EPOCHS,
    callbacks=[early_stopping],
    validation_data=(val_ds))
```
